NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
CHANGE OF NAME
Pramod, K. was born as a male child to Mr. Kochu, V., on 21st September 1983 residing at No. A4, Sriram Nagar,
2nd Street, Vyasarpadi, Chennai-600 039. After an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery she has been living as a female
(Reference Dr. Sanguan Kunaporn, M.D-Plastic Surgen, Phuket Plastic Surgery Center, 371/81, Yaowaraj Road, Muang,
Phuket 83000 Thailand). The Thorough clinical Examination under Dr. Dr. Sanguan Kunaporn, M.D., shows that I could be
treated as a female. Hence PRAMOD, K., shall be known as ASHA ELIZABETH PRAMOD.
Chennai-600 039,
27th May 2011.
